    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer15691201078902370885">This forthright narrative chronicles the author’s 1996 experiences as he adjusts to a massively transformed world. Emerging from 3 years in Saudi Arabia, and the 2 years prior cocooned in academia, he lands in Abu Dhabi to be hit with the triple-whammy of the NWO (1991), the WTO (1995), and the spigot of “India Inc.” opened wide. Considered too old (at 40) by his feminized</span>
  <span id="freeText15691201078902370885" style="display:none">This forthright narrative chronicles the author’s 1996 experiences as he adjusts to a massively transformed world. Emerging from 3 years in Saudi Arabia, and the 2 years prior cocooned in academia, he lands in Abu Dhabi to be hit with the triple-whammy of the NWO (1991), the WTO (1995), and the spigot of “India Inc.” opened wide. Considered too old (at 40) by his feminized native land, and too white-skinned by the Zio-Globalists, he must now face hostile (multicultural) politics and the economic subterfuge orbiting a liberal American empire dedicated to outsourcing and open borders.<br />Follow this Engineer’s eclectic adventures from the U.A.E., Malaysia, and England [Book-1] then on to India [Book-2] as he somehow negotiates a series of traps, obstacles, and near calamities while occasionally pausing to seduce a few of the world’s most exotic women.<br />This true, instructional, and entertaining testimony delivers a slew of lessons about how the 1990s cemented the fiscal and “chronically unemployed” quagmire plaguing the Western World since Y2K. Mesmerized by the “Clinton White House”, most people refused to listen back then. Twenty or more years on, could this book open your eyes now?</span>
  <a data-text-id="15691201078902370885" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2293444659?book_show_action=true">Feb 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="No Shelf Control" class="user" itemprop="url" name="No Shelf Control" href="/user/show/77684985-no-shelf-control">No Shelf Control</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2293444659" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14170312503264600995">“I have a habit of diverging strongly from what most might loosely call received wisdom. If a book cannot at least challenge opinions or pre-conceived ideas then why read it?”<br/><br/>I have the same feelings about books – sometimes I do want to step into a world of fantasy, but sometimes I want to be challenged, I want to learn from someone else's experiences and insights, and I want to hear a unique perspective. If you want the same, I urge you to pick up a copy of G. R. Wilson's unforgettable and comp</span>
  <span id="freeText14170312503264600995" style="display:none">“I have a habit of diverging strongly from what most might loosely call received wisdom. If a book cannot at least challenge opinions or pre-conceived ideas then why read it?”<br /><br />I have the same feelings about books – sometimes I do want to step into a world of fantasy, but sometimes I want to be challenged, I want to learn from someone else's experiences and insights, and I want to hear a unique perspective. If you want the same, I urge you to pick up a copy of G. R. Wilson's unforgettable and completely unique memoir. In a story worthy of TV serialization (I'm thinking Bryan Cranston to play Wilson), we travel through multiple continents, take on multiple interesting contracts, and hope for some sort of financial stability. Furthermore, get ready for some political insights that will blow your mind...the 1990's may have just ruined it for us Millenials. <br /><br />Well-written, well-informed ad so interesting and entertaining (seduction, beautiful women, corrupt cops, guns, and tropical locations), I highly recommend this memoir...I'm fairly certain it will be like nothing else you have ever read.<br /></span>

<div id="review_2303573241" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2303573241" />
    <a title="Literary Loft" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/78077927-literary-loft"><img alt="Literary Loft" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519225193p2/78077927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2303573241?book_show_action=true">Feb 21, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Literary Loft" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Literary Loft" href="/user/show/78077927-literary-loft">Literary Loft</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2303573241" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6270075938443161458">You can't turn on the news these days without hearing about debt (of countries, organisations and individuals), high levels of unemployment, and other issues that make you fearful for the future. We all know that these issues exist, but in 'Outsourced World' it is argued (very convincingly) that these modern issues have their roots back in the 1990's. With 'Slick Willy' in the White House, maybe that shouldn't have been such a surprise for me. <br/><br/>In his memoir 'Outsourced World', former engineer Gl</span>
  <span id="freeText6270075938443161458" style="display:none">You can't turn on the news these days without hearing about debt (of countries, organisations and individuals), high levels of unemployment, and other issues that make you fearful for the future. We all know that these issues exist, but in 'Outsourced World' it is argued (very convincingly) that these modern issues have their roots back in the 1990's. With 'Slick Willy' in the White House, maybe that shouldn't have been such a surprise for me. <br /><br />In his memoir 'Outsourced World', former engineer Glyn Wilson, entertains with tales of his experiences working overseas and quest for financial survival. He came under fire not once, but twice whilst in Baghdad, explored the Sahara desert, and was even robbed by police in Manilla (note to self, don't visit Manilla). But, he also manages to weave in important issues that defined the world of politics and economics in the vastly different 1990s. Lessons should have been learned, but they were not. If this continues, what world will we be facing 20 or 30 years from now.<br /><br />Just so you know, 'Slick Willy' wasn't the only one who was a hit with the ladies...Wilson certainly knew how to make the most of his time in those 24 countries. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6270075938443161458" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2279226118" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2279226118" />
    <a title="Biblio Fish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/77181618-biblio-fish"><img alt="Biblio Fish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517410664p2/77181618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2279226118?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Biblio Fish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Biblio Fish" href="/user/show/77181618-biblio-fish">Biblio Fish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2279226118" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10971541211578406809">In his preface, G. R, Wilson – author of Outsourced World – claims that men under the age of 50 of a similar background, will be inspired. Well I'm a woman in my 30s, with a wildly different background (I'm a freelancer that works primarily in her home office), but I still really loved book ,1 in his travel/work memoir trilogy Wilson is witty, thoughtful, insightful, and isn't afraid to stray into the controversial, and I admire that in a writer, particularly one of memoirs. It gives his work a </span>
  <span id="freeText10971541211578406809" style="display:none">In his preface, G. R, Wilson – author of Outsourced World – claims that men under the age of 50 of a similar background, will be inspired. Well I'm a woman in my 30s, with a wildly different background (I'm a freelancer that works primarily in her home office), but I still really loved book ,1 in his travel/work memoir trilogy Wilson is witty, thoughtful, insightful, and isn't afraid to stray into the controversial, and I admire that in a writer, particularly one of memoirs. It gives his work a realness and authenticity. We travel the world with Wilson, through his engineering career being outsourced to the likes of Jamaica, Saudi Arabia and even the Sahara desert. Through which he gained political and economical insights that are truly eye-opening. <br /><br />His author bio states that his focus is now on, amongst other things, cryptocurrencies, and I would love to know in uncensored thoughts on them. I will be reading more from Wilson in the future.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10971541211578406809" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4YKcjPRmQhgWVKFiJTO3cNO6gGh7YTIk+OXav5LnvEcZruhTDrQpmw39FbuB6bOnB3rEOa+VbTaCxumNcyEROw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('z97GjRCwdoo6Ub25N+JmuiUuZi6EAmZDKXmJiI/rKaU38rJS6mIdCSH4CWCTOGJt8e4if1D2OVFTWrq6bi2E2Q==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

This resulted in the deaths of over twenty thousand Roman soldiers. This in turn resulted in the Roman emperor called Tiberius recalling all Roman military units from Germania. The Germanic tribes would associate for their common good, often meeting and forming up for offensive or defensive war, but they were always separate and very independent. Armin knew that the best way to ensure that his country was not bothered by outside invaders again was to become a single country complete with it own army and navy. In this he crossed swords with the independent temper of his own people. They did not want any king from anywhere telling them what to do. In due course, this resulted in even the members of his own family taking up arms against him in order to make sure that the tribes of Germania remained independent and free. Snyder did when he joined it;• German atrocities toward captured crew and civilians;• behind-the-scenes stories of the Belgium civilians who risked all to save American flyers who were in the air one moment, spiraling down in flames the next;• creation and dedication of the monument to the Susan Ruth and its crew located in Macquenoise, Belgium in 1989.Shot Down was created from the vast number of letters and journals of Howard Snyder; diaries of men and women on the ground who rescued, sheltered and hid the crew; and interviews conducted by historians. Centered around the 306th Bomb Group in Thurleigh, England, it is informative, insightful and captivating.For most, 70 years is a long time ago. World War II fades in importance as each year goes by. Shot Down moves history out of the footnotes into reality, keeping the stories of real people alive as they experience being shot down. You are there, almost holding your breath as Lt. <span id="freeTextContainer757670545990015451">Born in northwest England, Glyn Rodney Wilson is a Licensed Engineer (Controls & Instrumentation) who has worked for some of the world's major companies, including: Unilever, British Nuclear Fuels (BNFL), Alcan, Saudi-Aramco, Yanpet, Occidental Petroleum, Bechtel, and Repsol.<br/><br/>Since January 1980 he has visited 22 countries (or 24 distinct territories) and worked in 9 of those ... including: Holland,</span>
  <span id="freeText757670545990015451" style="display:none">Born in northwest England, Glyn Rodney Wilson is a Licensed Engineer (Controls &amp; Instrumentation) who has worked for some of the world's major companies, including: Unilever, British Nuclear Fuels (BNFL), Alcan, Saudi-Aramco, Yanpet, Occidental Petroleum, Bechtel, and Repsol.<br /><br />Since January 1980 he has visited 22 countries (or 24 distinct territories) and worked in 9 of those ... including: Holland, all littoral Arabian Gulf countries (except Kuwait &amp; Iran), India, Iraq, Libya, and Jamaica.<br /><br />Glyn holds various technical qualifications, plus a Master of Science (MSc) Degree in “Artificial Intelligence with Engineering Applications”, gained (1994) with a leading UK (Russell Group) university.<br /><br />Prior to authoring the book title(s) listed here in Goodreads, Glyn has also earned a living both as a Curriculum Developer, and Technical Author ... producing complex documents such as:<br /><br />+ Illustrated training manuals for Saudi Arabia's premier utility company;<br />+ Technical training courses (curricula) for Abu Dhabi's State-Owned oil company;<br />+ Operator Procedures for the world's largest NGL plant (in Ras Laffan, Qatar);<br />+ Illustrated marketing manual, in colour, for Exxon-Mobil in Doha (Qatar).</span>

This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
